<summary>actuallyadditions/lamp_controller</summary>

```diff
+{
+  type: "minecraft:crafting_shaped"
+  category: "misc"
+  key: {
+    L: {
+      tag: "actuallyadditions:lamps"
+    }
+    R: {
+      item: "actuallyadditions:restonia_crystal"
+    }
+  }
+  pattern: [
+    "RRR"
+    "RLR"
+    "RRR"
+  ]
+  result: {
+    count: 4
+    id: "actuallyadditions:lamp_controller"
+  }
+}

```

+                  predicate: {
+                    items: "minecraft:netherite_hoe"
+                  }
+                }

+                  chance: 0.04
+                  condition: "minecraft:random_chance"

+                    items: "minecraft:diamond_hoe"
+                  }
+                }
